class="">Yeh tumhare shared documents (“Pizza Sales PPT” aur “PIZZA SALES SQL QUERIES”) se maine jo “content details” aur KPIs identify kiye hain, unka ek structured overview yeh raha:</p>
<hr data-start="177" data-end="180" class="">
<h2 data-start="182" data-end="226" class="">1. Project Overview &amp; Problem Statement</h2>
<ul data-start="227" data-end="455">
<li data-start="227" data-end="455" class="">
<p data-start="229" data-end="455" class=""><strong data-start="229" data-end="242">Objective</strong>: Pizza sales data ko analyze karke business performance ke key indicators nikalna, trends identify karna, aur actionable insights dena. </p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="457" data-end="460" class="">
<h2 data-start="462" data-end="479" class="">2. Core KPIs</h2>
<ol data-start="480" data-end="1673">
<li data-start="480" data-end="688" class="">
<p data-start="483" data-end="502" class=""><strong data-start="483" data-end="500">Total Revenue</strong></p>
<ul data-start="506" data-end="688">
<li data-start="506" data-end="540" class="">
<p data-start="508" data-end="540" class="">Sum of all orders’ total_price</p>
</li>
<li data-start="544" data-end="688" class="">
<p data-start="546" data-end="688" class="">SQL: <code data-start="551" data-end="611">SELECT SUM(total_price) AS Total_Revenue FROM pizza_sales;</code> </p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="689" data-end="912" class="">
<p data-start="692" data-end="717" class=""><strong data-start="692" data-end="715">Average Order Value</strong></p>
<ul data-start="721" data-end="912">
<li data-start="721" data-end="753" class="">
<p data-start="723" data-end="753" class="">Total Revenue ÷ Total Orders</p>
</li>
<li data-start="757" data-end="912" class="">
<p data-start="759" data-end="912" class="">SQL: <code data-start="764" data-end="835">SELECT SUM(total_price)/COUNT(DISTINCT order_id) AS Avg_order_Value …</code> </p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="913" data-end="1116" class="">
<p data-start="916" data-end="939" class=""><strong data-start="916" data-end="937">Total Pizzas Sold</strong></p>
<ul data-start="943" data-end="1116">
<li data-start="943" data-end="968" class="">
<p data-start="945" data-end="968" class="">Sum of all quantities</p>
</li>
<li data-start="972" data-end="1116" class="">
<p data-start="974" data-end="1116" class="">SQL: <code data-start="979" data-end="1039">SELECT SUM(quantity) AS Total_pizza_sold FROM pizza_sales;</code> </p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1117" data-end="1327" class="">
<p data-start="1120" data-end="1138" class=""><strong data-start="1120" data-end="1136">Total Orders</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1142" data-end="1327">
<li data-start="1142" data-end="1172" class="">
<p data-start="1144" data-end="1172" class="">Count of distinct order_id</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1176" data-end="1327" class="">
<p data-start="1178" data-end="1327" class="">SQL: <code data-start="1183" data-end="1250">SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT order_id) AS Total_Orders FROM pizza_sales;</code> </p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1328" data-end="1673" class="">
<p data-start="1331" data-end="1361" class=""><strong data-start="1331" data-end="1359">Average Pizzas Per Order</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1365" data-end="1673">
<li data-start="1365" data-end="1401" class="">
<p data-start="1367" data-end="1401" class="">Total Pizzas Sold ÷ Total Orders</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1405" data-end="1673" class="">
<p data-start="1407" data-end="1441" class="">SQL uses a CAST to two decimals:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="1447" data-end="1673"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary" </span></span></code></div></div></pre>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="1674" data-end="1677" class="">
<h2 data-start="1679" data-end="1713" class="">3. Visualization Requirements</h2>
<ul data-start="1714" data-end="3086">
<li data-start="1714" data-end="1895" class="">
<p data-start="1716" data-end="1756" class=""><strong data-start="1716" data-end="1754">Hourly Trend for Total Pizzas Sold</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1759" data-end="1895">
<li data-start="1759" data-end="1895" class="">
<p data-start="1761" data-end="1895" class="">Stacked bar chart of pizzas sold by each hour (0–23). </p>
</li>

<li data-start="1896" data-end="2081" class="">
<p data-start="1898" data-end="1933" class=""><strong data-start="1898" data-end="1931">Weekly Trend for Total Orders</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1936" data-end="2081">
<li data-start="1936" data-end="2081" class="">
<p data-start="1938" data-end="2081" class="">Line chart showing ISO week-by-week total orders for the year. </p>

<li data-start="2082" data-end="2299" class="">

&lt;h1 align="center"&gt;🍕 Pizza Sales Dashboard By Harsh Wadiya 📊&lt;/h1&gt;

&lt;p align="center"&gt;
  A complete SQL + Tableau  project to uncover insights from pizza sales data.&lt;br&gt;
  &lt;strong&gt;Technologies:&lt;/strong&gt; MySQL • Tableau • Data Visualization
&lt;/p&gt;

---

## 📁 Table of Contents
- [📌 Project Objective](#-project-objective)
- [📊 KPI &amp; Metrics](#-kpi--metrics)
- [📁 Data Cleaning](#-data-cleaning)
- [🧮 SQL Queries](#-sql-queries)
- [📈 Tableau Dashboards](#-tableau-dashboards)
- [🧠 Tools Used](#-tools-used)
- [📚 References](#-references)

---

## 🚀 Live Demo

🔍 **Click on the image below to explore the live demo of the Pizza Sales Dashboard:**

[![Click here to view the Live Demo - Pizza Sales Dashboard](https://github.com/harshwadiya/Pizza_sales_Dashboard/blob/30d15293111918dc5530c64361907a97a2b78e6a/Key%20Insights%20and%20Dashboard/Dashboard%20Home%201.png)](https://public.tableau.com/app/profile/harsh.wadiya/viz/PizzaSalesDashBoard_17454720470660/HOME)

🔗 **Or directly visit the demo via this [🔗 link](https://public.tableau.com/app/profile/harsh.wadiya/viz/PizzaSalesDashBoard_17454720470660/HOME)**.

✨ **Explore the interactive and insightful data visualizations now!**


---

## 📌 Project Objective

The aim is to analyze pizza sales to:
- Identify peak sales hours and days.
- Understand performance by pizza size and category.
- Find top-selling and underperforming pizzas.
- Generate visually rich reports using Tableau for business decision-making.

---

## 📊 KPI &amp; Metrics

| Metric | Description |
|--------|-------------|
| **Total Revenue** | Total earnings from all sales |
| **Average Order Value** | Revenue ÷ Number of Orders |
| **Total Pizzas Sold** | Sum of all pizza quantities |
| **Total Orders** | Unique customer orders |
| **Avg Pizzas per Order** | Pizzas ÷ Orders |

---

## 📁 Data Cleaning

✔ Abbreviations of pizza sizes were converted for clarity in Tableau dashboard:  
<code>S → Small</code>, <code>M → Medium</code>, <code>L → Large</code>, <code>XL → Extra Large</code>, <code>XXL → Jumbo</code>.

<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>sql
SELECT pizza_size,
  CASE
    WHEN pizza_size = 'S' THEN 'Small'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'M' THEN 'Medium'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'L' THEN 'Large'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'XL' THEN 'Extra Large'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'XXL' THEN 'Jumbo'
  END AS full_size
FROM pizza_sales;</code></pre>

---

## 🧮 SQL Queries

Below are key SQL queries used to generate insights:

### 📌 Key Performance Indicators

<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>sql
-- Total Revenue
SELECT SUM(total_price) AS total_revenue FROM pizza_sales;

-- Average Order Value
SELECT SUM(total_price) / COUNT(DISTINCT order_id) AS avg_order_value FROM pizza_sales;

-- Total Pizzas Sold
SELECT SUM(quantity) AS total_pizza_sold FROM pizza_sales;

-- Total Orders
SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT order_id) AS total_orders FROM pizza_sales;

-- Average Pizzas Per Order
SELECT ROUND(SUM(quantity) / COUNT(DISTINCT order_id), 2) AS avg_pizza_per_order FROM pizza_sales;</code></pre>

### 📈 Trend Analysis

<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>sql
-- Hourly Sales Trend
SELECT HOUR(order_time) AS hour, SUM(quantity) AS pizzas_sold
FROM pizza_sales
GROUP BY hour ORDER BY hour;

-- Weekly Orders
SELECT WEEK(order_date, 3) AS week, COUNT(DISTINCT order_id) AS orders
FROM pizza_sales
GROUP BY week ORDER BY week;</code></pre>

### 🍕 Category &amp; Size Analysis

<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>sql
-- % Sales by Category
SELECT pizza_category,
  ROUND(SUM(total_price) * 100 / (SELECT SUM(total_price) FROM pizza_sales), 2) AS pct
FROM pizza_sales GROUP BY pizza_category;

-- % Sales by Size
SELECT pizza_size,
  ROUND(SUM(total_price), 2) AS revenue
FROM pizza_sales GROUP BY pizza_size ORDER BY pizza_size;</code></pre>

### 🥇 Top &amp; Bottom Pizzas

<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>sql
-- Top 5 by Revenue
SELECT pizza_name, SUM(total_price) AS revenue
FROM pizza_sales GROUP BY pizza_name ORDER BY revenue DESC LIMIT 5;

-- Bottom 5 by Orders
SELECT pizza_name, COUNT(DISTINCT order_id) AS orders
FROM pizza_sales GROUP BY pizza_name ORDER BY orders ASC LIMIT 5;</code></pre>

---

<ul data-start="63" data-end="499">
<li data-start="63" data-end="171" class="">
<p data-start="65" data-end="171" class="">Yeh ek “Plato’s Pizza Project” hai, hosted on RPubs by Ryann Laky. <span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://rpubs.com/ryannlaky/983451" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[0.5625em] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">RPubs</span></span></span></a></span></p>
</li>
<li data-start="172" data-end="323" class="">
<p data-start="174" data-end="323" class="">Page last updated “over 2 years ago” hai, aur yeh RStudio/R Markdown se banā ek interactive report lagtā hai. <span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://rpubs.com/ryannlaky/983451" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[0.5625em] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">RPubs</span></span></span></a></span></p>
</li>
<li data-start="324" data-end="499" class="">
<p data-start="326" data-end="499" class="">Naam se pratit hotā hai ki yahan pizza sales ki data import, cleaning, exploration aur visualizations (charts/plots) diye gaye honge. <span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://rpubs.com/ryannlaky/983451" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[0.5625em] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">RPubs</span></span></span></a></span></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="501" data-end="753" class="">Filhaal page ka detailed content without login visible nahin ho pāyā, lekin overall structure ek complete analytics report dikhatī hai, jisme sections jaise Data Loading, Cleaning, KPI Calculation, Trend Analysis, aur Visual Dashboards ho sakte hain.</p>
<p data-start="755" data-end="882" class=""><strong data-start="755" data-end="764">Next:</strong> Bataiye agar aapko is inspiration example se koi specific details chahiye, ya phir main aage ka content gather karun.</p>

bis_skin_checked="1"><hr></div><h2><span>📌 Project Overview</span></h2><p><span><strong>Objective:</strong></span><span> Analyse pizza sales data to identify peak hours/days, performance by pizza size and category, top and underperforming pizzas, and provide actionable insights through interactive dashboards for stakeholder validation.</span></p><p><span><strong>Stakeholder Validation:</strong></span><span> Included SQL queries for calculating KPIs and trends to ensure findings can be independently verified by stakeholders.</span></p><div contenteditable="false" bis_skin_checked="1"><hr></div><h2><span>📊 KPI &amp; Metrics</span></h2><table><tbody><tr><th><span>Metric</span></th><th><span>Description</span></th></tr><tr><td><span><strong>Total Revenue</strong></span></td><td><span>Total earnings from all sales</span></td></tr><tr><td><span><strong>Average Order Value</strong></span></td><td><span>Revenue ÷ Number of Orders</span></td></tr><tr><td><span><strong>Total Pizzas Sold</strong></span></td><td><span>Sum of all pizza quantities</span></td></tr><tr><td><span><strong>Total Orders</strong></span></td><td><span>Unique customer orders</span></td></tr><tr><td><span><strong>Avg Pizzas per Order</strong></span></td><td><span>Pizzas ÷ Orders</span></td></tr></tbody></table><p><span><strong>Dashboard Screenshot:</strong></span></p><div contenteditable="false" bis_skin_checked="1"><hr></div><h2><span>📁 Data Cleaning</span></h2><ul </span><span><span class="hljs-section">## 📌 Project Overview</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Objective:**</span></span><span> Analyse pizza sales data to identify peak hours/days, performance by pizza size and category, top and underperforming pizzas, and provide actionable insights through interactive dashboards for stakeholder validation.

</span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Stakeholder Validation:**</span></span><span> Included SQL queries for calculating KPIs and trends to ensure findings can be independently verified by stakeholders.

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## 📊 KPI &amp; Metrics</span></span><span>

| Metric                  | Description                        |
|-------------------------|------------------------------------|
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Revenue**</span></span><span>       | Total earnings from all sales      |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Average Order Value**</span></span><span> | Revenue ÷ Number of Orders         |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Pizzas Sold**</span></span><span>   | Sum of all pizza quantities        |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Orders**</span></span><span>        | Unique customer orders             |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Avg Pizzas per Order**</span></span><span>| Pizzas ÷ Orders                    |

</span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Dashboard Screenshot:**</span></span><span>

&lt;!-- Insert image: Dashboard</span><span><span class="hljs-emphasis">_Home_</span></span><span>1<span class="hljs-emphasis">_KPIs.png --&gt;

---

## 📁 Data Cleaning

- Converted size abbreviations for clarity:
  ```sql
  SELECT pizza_</span>size,
<span class="hljs-code">    CASE
      WHEN pizza_size = 'S' THEN 'Small'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'M' THEN 'Medium'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'L' THEN 'Large'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'XL' THEN 'Extra Large'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'XXL' THEN 'Jumbo'
    END AS full_size
  FROM pizza_sales;
</span></span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="1965" data-end="1968" class="">
<h2 data-start="1970" data-end="1987" class="">🧮 SQL Queries</h2>
<h3 data-start="1989" data-end="2007" class="">A. KPI Queries</h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="2008" data-end="2500"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary" bis_skin_checked="1"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none rounded-t-[5px]" bis_skin_checked="1">sql</div><div class="sticky top-9" bis_skin_checked="1"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2" bis_skin_checked="1"><div class="bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary flex items-center rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs" bis_skin_checked="1"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none px-4 py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-xs"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy</button></span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex items-center gap-1 px-4 py-1 select-none"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-xs"><path d="M2.5 5.5C4.3 5.2 5.2 4 5.5 2.5C5.8 4 6.7 5.2 8.5 5.5C6.7 5.8 5.8 7 5.5 8.5C5.2 7 4.3 5.8 2.5 5.5Z" fill="currentColor" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M5.66282 16.5231L5.18413 19.3952C5.12203 19.7678 5.09098 19.9541 5.14876 20.0888C5.19933 20.2067 5.29328 20.3007 5.41118 20.3512C5.54589 20.409 5.73218 20.378 6.10476 20.3159L8.97693 19.8372C9.72813 19.712 10.1037 19.6494 10.4542 19.521C10.7652 19.407 11.0608 19.2549 11.3343 19.068C11.6425 18.8575 11.9118 18.5882 12.4503 18.0497L20 10.5C21.3807 9.11929 21.3807 6.88071 20 5.5C18.6193 4.11929 16.3807 4.11929 15 5.5L7.45026 13.0497C6.91175 13.5882 6.6425 13.8575 6.43197 14.1657C6.24513 14.4392 6.09299 14.7348 5.97903 15.0458C5.85062 15.3963 5.78802 15.7719 5.66282 16.5231Z" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M14.5 7L18.5 11" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg>Edit</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr" bis_skin_checked="1"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-sql"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Total Revenue</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(total_price) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Total_Revenue
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Average Order Value</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(total_price) </span><span><span class="hljs-operator">/</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">COUNT</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">DISTINCT</span></span><span> order_id) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Avg_Order_Value
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Total Pizzas Sold</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(quantity) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Total_Pizzas_Sold
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Total Orders</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">COUNT</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">DISTINCT</span></span><span> order_id) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Total_Orders
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Average Pizzas Per Order</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> ROUND(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(quantity) </span><span><span class="hljs-operator">/</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">COUNT</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">DISTINCT</span></span><span> order_id), </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Avg_Pizzas_Per_Order
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

bis_skin_checked="1"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-markdown"><span><span>🍕 Pizza Sales Dashboard 📊

</span><span><span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span></span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-attr">align</span></span><span>=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"center"</span></span><span>&gt;
  A complete SQL + Tableau project to uncover insights from pizza sales data.</span><span><span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">br</span></span></span></span><span>&gt;
  </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Technologies:**</span></span><span> MySQL • Tableau • Data Visualization
</span><span><span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span></span></span></span><span>&gt;

</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">5.</span></span><span> [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">📈 Tableau Dashboards</span></span><span>](</span><span><span class="hljs-link">#-tableau-dashboards</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">7.</span></span><span> [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">📚 References</span></span><span>](</span><span><span class="hljs-link">#-references</span></span><span>)

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## 📌 Project Overview</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Objective:**</span></span><span> Analyse pizza sales data to identify peak hours/days, performance by pizza size and category, top and underperforming pizzas, and provide actionable insights through interactive dashboards for stakeholder validation.

</span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Stakeholder Validation:**</span></span><span> Included SQL queries for calculating KPIs and trends to ensure findings can be independently verified by stakeholders.

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## 📊 KPI &amp; Metrics</span></span><span>

| Metric                  | Description                        |
|-------------------------|------------------------------------|
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Revenue**</span></span><span>       | Total earnings from all sales      |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Average Order Value**</span></span><span> | Revenue ÷ Number of Orders         |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Pizzas Sold**</span></span><span>   | Sum of all pizza quantities        |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Orders**</span></span><span>        | Unique customer orders             |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Avg Pizzas per Order**</span></span><span>| Pizzas ÷ Orders                    |

</span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Dashboard Screenshot:**</span></span><span>

&lt;!-- Insert image: Dashboard</span><span><span class="hljs-emphasis">_Home_</span></span><span>1<span class="hljs-emphasis">_KPIs.png --&gt;

---

## 📁 Data Cleaning

- Converted size abbreviations for clarity:
  ```sql
  SELECT pizza_</span>size,
<span class="hljs-code">    CASE
      WHEN pizza_size = 'S' THEN 'Small'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'M' THEN 'Medium'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'L' THEN 'Large'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'XL' THEN 'Extra Large'
      WHEN pizza_size = 'XXL' THEN 'Jumbo'
    END AS full_size
  FROM pizza_sales;
</span></span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="1965" data-end="1968" class="">
<h2 data-start="1970" data-end="1987" class="">🧮 SQL Queries</h2>

class="hljs-comment">-- Total Revenue</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## 📌 Project Overview</span></span><span>

The goal of this project is to analyze a year’s worth of pizza sales data and uncover key business insights using SQL and Tableau. The dashboard helps stakeholders understand:
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Peak sales hours and days
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Best and worst performing pizzas
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Performance by size and category
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Weekly and hourly trends
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Sales contribution by category and size

This README includes SQL queries used for stakeholder validation and clear visualizations with image placeholders.

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## 📊 KPI &amp; Metrics</span></span><span>

| Metric | Description |
|--------|-------------|
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Revenue**</span></span><span> | Total earnings from all sales |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Average Order Value**</span></span><span> | Revenue ÷ Number of Orders |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Pizzas Sold**</span></span><span> | Sum of all pizza quantities |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Total Orders**</span></span><span> | Unique customer orders |
| </span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**Avg Pizzas per Order**</span></span><span> | Pizzas ÷ Orders |

</span><span><span class="hljs-strong">**📸 KPI Visual**</span></span><span>  
&lt;!-- Insert image: Dashboard</span><span><span class="hljs-emphasis">_Home_</span></span><span>1<span class="hljs-emphasis">_KPIs.png --&gt;

---

## 📁 Data Cleaning

Simplified pizza size names for clarity in Tableau:
```sql
SELECT pizza_</span>size,
  CASE
<span class="hljs-code">    WHEN pizza_size = 'S' THEN 'Small'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'M' THEN 'Medium'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'L' THEN 'Large'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'XL' THEN 'Extra Large'
    WHEN pizza_size = 'XXL' THEN 'Jumbo'
  END AS full_size
FROM pizza_sales;
</span></span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="2053" data-end="2056" class="">
<h2 data-start="2058" data-end="2075" class="">🧮 SQL Queries</h2>
<h3 data-start="2077" data-end="2095" class="">📌 KPI Queries</h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="2096" data-end="2584"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary" bis_skin_checked="1"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none rounded-t-[5px]" bis_skin_checked="1">sql</div><div class="sticky top-9" bis_skin_checked="1"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2" bis_skin_checked="1"><div class="bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary flex items-center rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs" bis_skin_checked="1"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none px-4 py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-xs"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy</button></span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex items-center gap-1 px-4 py-1 select-none"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-xs"><path d="M2.5 5.5C4.3 5.2 5.2 4 5.5 2.5C5.8 4 6.7 5.2 8.5 5.5C6.7 5.8 5.8 7 5.5 8.5C5.2 7 4.3 5.8 2.5 5.5Z" fill="currentColor" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M5.66282 16.5231L5.18413 19.3952C5.12203 19.7678 5.09098 19.9541 5.14876 20.0888C5.19933 20.2067 5.29328 20.3007 5.41118 20.3512C5.54589 20.409 5.73218 20.378 6.10476 20.3159L8.97693 19.8372C9.72813 19.712 10.1037 19.6494 10.4542 19.521C10.7652 19.407 11.0608 19.2549 11.3343 19.068C11.6425 18.8575 11.9118 18.5882 12.4503 18.0497L20 10.5C21.3807 9.11929 21.3807 6.88071 20 5.5C18.6193 4.11929 16.3807 4.11929 15 5.5L7.45026 13.0497C6.91175 13.5882 6.6425 13.8575 6.43197 14.1657C6.24513 14.4392 6.09299 14.7348 5.97903 15.0458C5.85062 15.3963 5.78802 15.7719 5.66282 16.5231Z" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M14.5 7L18.5 11" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg>Edit</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr" bis_skin_checked="1"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-sql"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Total Revenue</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(total_price) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Total_Revenue </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Average Order Value</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(total_price)</span><span><span class="hljs-operator">/</span></span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">COUNT</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">DISTINCT</span></span><span> order_id) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Avg_Order_Value </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Total Pizzas Sold</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(quantity) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Total_Pizzas_Sold </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Total Orders</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">COUNT</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">DISTINCT</span></span><span> order_id) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Total_Orders </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Average Pizzas Per Order</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> ROUND(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(quantity)</span><span><span class="hljs-operator">/</span></span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">COUNT</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">DISTINCT</span></span><span> order_id), </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Avg_Pizzas_Per_Order </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales;
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

class="hljs-comment">-- Hourly Sales Trend</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> DATEPART(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">HOUR</span></span><span>, order_time) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">Hour</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(quantity) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Pizzas_Sold
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">GROUP</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">BY</span></span><span> DATEPART(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">HOUR</span></span><span>, order_time)
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">ORDER</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">BY</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">Hour</span></span><span>;

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">-- Weekly Orders</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> DATEPART(ISO_WEEK, order_date) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> WeekNumber, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">COUNT</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">DISTINCT</span></span><span> order_id) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Orders
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">FROM</span></span><span> pizza_sales </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">GROUP</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">BY</span></span><span> DATEPART(ISO_WEEK, order_date)
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">ORDER</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">BY</span></span><span> WeekNumber;
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<h3 data-start="2965" data-end="2997" class="">🍕 Category &amp; Size Breakdown</h3>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">SELECT</span></span><span> TOP </span><span><span class="hljs-number">5</span></span><span> pizza_name, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">SUM</span></span><span>(total_price) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">AS</span></span><span> Revenue
